41→\t// 'pods' means pods.\n    42→\t// 'pods/log' means the log subresource of pods.\n    43→\t// '*' means all resources, but not subresources.\n    44→\t// 'pods/*' means all subresources of pods.\n    45→\t// '*/scale' means all scale subresources.\n    46→\t// '*/*' means all resources and their subresources.\n    47→\t//\n    48→\t// If wildcard is present, the validation rule will The `Webhook` struct (webhook.go:50) orchestrates the entire admission process and implements the `admission.Interface`. It uses a factory pattern with `sourceFactory` and `dispatcherFactory` to support different webhook types. The `NewWebhook` function (webhook.go:73) initializes the webhook with a client manager, namespace matcher, object matcher, and dispatcher. The `ShouldCallHook` method (webhook.go:158) determines whether to invoke a specific webhook by evaluating namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions. The core `Dispatch` method (webhook.go:255) gets the list of webhooks from the source and delegates to the specific dispatcher.\\n\\nThe `generic/interfaces.go` file defines the critical `Dispatcher` interface (line 47) which all webhook dispatchers must implement. It takes admission attributes and objects along with a list of webhooks and returns an error if the request should be rejected. The `WebhookInvocation` struct (line 39) describes how to call a webhook, including the webhook accessor, resource, subresource, and kind. The `Source` interface (line 32) provides dynamic webhook listings.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Dispatcher\\n\\nThe mutating webhook dispatcher at `kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go` implements sequential webhook invocation with support for reinvocation. The `mutatingDispatcher` struct (line 68) holds the client manager and plugin reference. The `Dispatch` method (line 105) is the key entry point that:\\n\\n1. Retrieves or creates a `webhookReinvokeContext` from the admission attributes (lines 106-113)\\n2. Checks if the object has changed since the last webhook invocation and triggers reinvocation if needed (lines 115-119)\\n3. Iterates through hooks sequentially, calling `ShouldCallHook` to filter relevant ones (lines 127-139)\\n4. For each hook that should be invoked, calls `callAttrMutatingHook` (line 166)\\n5. Tracks which webhooks mutated the object and requires reinvocation if mutations occurred (lines 192-195)\\n6. When set to \\\"IfNeeded\\\", the webhook may be called multiple times if other plugins modify the object.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Dispatcher\\n\\nThe validating webhook dispatcher at `kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go` implements parallel webhook invocation for efficiency. The `validatingDispatcher` struct (line 55) is similar to the mutating dispatcher but with different dispatch behavior.\\n\\nThe `Dispatch` method (line 88) performs parallel validation by:\\n\\n1. Collecting errors from all goroutines and returning the first error if validation fails (lines 232-245)\\n\\nThe `callHook` method (line 248) is similar to the mutating version but does not apply patches or track mutations, only validates the object.\\n\\nKey differences from mutating dispatchers:\\n- Parallel execution using goroutines (line 129-227)\\n- Separate `versionedAttributeAccessor` using a map to cache multiple versions (lines 68-84)\\n- Panic recovery and error collection through a channel (line 127)\\n- No reinvocation logic or object modification tracking\\n\\n## WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface (kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go, line 37) provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks. Name, ClientConfig, Rules for routing\\n  - FailurePolicy (Ignore or Fail)\\n  - MatchPolicy (Exact or Equivalent)\\n  - Selectors for namespace and objects\\n  - SideEffects declaration\\n  - TimeoutSeconds and AdmissionReviewVersions\\n  - `kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/`. The `Webhook` struct (webhook.go:50) orchestrates the entire admission process and implements the `admission.Interface`. It uses a factory pattern with `sourceFactory` and `dispatcherFactory` to support different webhook types. The `NewWebhook` function (webhook.go:73) initializes the webhook with a client manager, namespace matcher, object matcher, and dispatcher. The `ShouldCallHook` method (webhook.go:158) determines whether to invoke a specific webhook by evaluating namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions. The core `Dispatch` method (webhook.go:255) gets the list of webhooks from the source and delegates to the specific dispatcher.\\n\\nThe `generic/interfaces.go` file defines the critical `Dispatcher` interface (line 47) which all webhook dispatchers must implement. It takes admission attributes and objects along with a list of webhooks and returns an error if the request should be rejected. The `WebhookInvocation` struct (line 39) describes how to call a webhook, including the webhook accessor, resource, subresource, and kind. The `Source` interface (line 32) provides dynamic webhook listings.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Dispatcher\\n\\nThe mutating webhook dispatcher at `kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go` implements sequential webhook invocation with support for reinvocation. The `mutatingDispatcher` struct (line 68) holds the client manager and plugin reference. The `Dispatch` method (line 105) is the key entry point that:\\n\\n1. Retrieves or creates a `webhookReinvokeContext` from the admission attributes (lines 106-113)\\n2. Checks if the object has changed since the last webhook invocation and triggers reinvocation if needed (lines 115-119)\\n3. Iterates through hooks sequentially, calling `ShouldCallHook` to filter relevant ones (lines 127-139)\\n4. For each hook that should be invoked, calls `callAttrMutatingHook` (line 166)\\n5. When set to \\\"IfNeeded\\\", the webhook may be called multiple times if other plugins modify the object.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Dispatcher\\n\\nThe validating webhook dispatcher at `kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go` implements parallel webhook invocation for efficiency. The `validatingDispatcher` struct (line 55) is similar to the mutating dispatcher but with different dispatch behavior.\\n\\nThe `Dispatch` method (line 88) performs parallel validation by:\\n\\n1. Pre-computing versioned attributes for all relevant webhooks (lines 106-110)\\n3. Creating a wait group and spawning goroutines for each webhook (lines 126-228)\\n4. Each goroutine calls `callHook` independently with proper error recovery and panic handling (lines 130-227)\\n5. Collecting errors from all goroutines and returning the first error if validation fails (lines 232-245)\\n\\nThe `callHook` method (line 248) is similar to the mutating version but does not apply patches or track mutations, only validates the object.\\n\\nKey differences from mutating dispatchers:\\n- Parallel execution using goroutines (line 129-227)\\n- Separate `versionedAttributeAccessor` using a map to cache multiple versions (lines 68-84)\\n- Panic recovery and error collection through a channel (line 127)\\n- No reinvocation logic or object modification tracking\\n\\n## WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface (kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go, line 37) provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks. Pre-computing versioned attributes for all relevant webhooks (lines 106-110)\\n3. Creating a wait group and spawning goroutines for each webhook (lines 126-228)\\n4. Each goroutine calls `callHook` independently with proper error recovery and panic handling (lines 130-227)\\n5. Collecting errors from all goroutines and returning the first error if validation fails (lines 232-245)\\n\\nThe `callHook` method (line 248) is similar to the mutating version but does not apply patches or track mutations, only validates the object.\\n\\nKey differences from mutating dispatchers:\\n- Parallel execution using goroutines (line 129-227)\\n- Separate `versionedAttributeAccessor` using a map to cache multiple versions (lines 68-84)\\n- Panic recovery and error collection through a channel (line 127)\\n- No reinvocation logic or object modification tracking\\n\\n## WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface (kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go, line 37) provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks.
